IR_check_good_prices = {
	#
	event_target:grain_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 1 } }
	event_target:wine_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 1 } }
	event_target:wool_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 1 } }
	event_target:cloth_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 1 } }
	event_target:fish_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 1 } }

	event_target:dyes_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 1 } }
	event_target:livestock_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 1 } }
	event_target:incense_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 1 } }
	event_target:glass_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 1 } }
	event_target:gems_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 1 } }
	event_target:paper_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 1 } }
	event_target:beer_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 1 } }
	event_target:books_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 1 } }
	event_target:rice_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 1 } }
	event_target:whales_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 1 } }
	event_target:silver_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 1 } }
	event_target:potato_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 1 } }
	event_target:maize_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 1 } }
	event_target:millet_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 1 } }
	event_target:apiculture_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 1 } }
	event_target:fruit_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 1 } }
	event_target:olives_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 1 } }
	event_target:dates_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 1 } }
	event_target:marble_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 1 } }
	event_target:softwood_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 1 } }
	#
	every_country = {
		limit = { trading_bonus = { trade_goods = grain value = yes } }
		if = { 
			limit = { production_leader = { trade_goods = grain } }
			if 		= { limit = { trading_part = { trade_goods = grain value = 1.0 } } change_price = { trade_goods = grain key = 100P_CONSOLIDATION value = 4 duration = 364 } event_target:grain_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 5 } } }
			else_if = { limit = { trading_part = { trade_goods = grain value = 0.9 } } change_price = { trade_goods = grain key = 90P_CONSOLIDATION value = 3.9 duration = 364 } event_target:grain_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 4.9 } } }
			else_if = { limit = { trading_part = { trade_goods = grain value = 0.8 } } change_price = { trade_goods = grain key = 80P_CONSOLIDATION value = 3.75 duration = 364 } event_target:grain_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 4.75 } } }
			else_if = { limit = { trading_part = { trade_goods = grain value = 0.7 } } change_price = { trade_goods = grain key = 70P_CONSOLIDATION value = 3.5 duration = 364 } event_target:grain_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 4.5 } } }
			else_if = { limit = { trading_part = { trade_goods = grain value = 0.6 } } change_price = { trade_goods = grain key = 60P_CONSOLIDATION value = 3 duration = 364 } event_target:grain_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 4 } } }
			else_if = { limit = { trading_part = { trade_goods = grain value = 0.5 } } change_price = { trade_goods = grain key = 50P_CONSOLIDATION value = 2 duration = 364 } event_target:grain_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 3 } } }
			else_if = { limit = { trading_part = { trade_goods = grain value = 0.4 } } change_price = { trade_goods = grain key = 40P_CONSOLIDATION value = 1 duration = 364 } event_target:grain_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 2 } } }
			else_if = { limit = { trading_part = { trade_goods = grain value = 0.3 } } change_price = { trade_goods = grain key = 30P_CONSOLIDATION value = 0.5 duration = 364 } event_target:grain_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 1.5 } } }
			else_if = { limit = { trading_part = { trade_goods = grain value = 0.2 } } change_price = { trade_goods = grain key = 20P_CONSOLIDATION value = 0.25 duration = 364 } event_target:grain_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 1.25 } } }
			else_if = { limit = { trading_part = { trade_goods = grain value = 0.1 } } change_price = { trade_goods = grain key = 10P_CONSOLIDATION value = 0.1 duration = 364 } event_target:grain_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 1.1 } } }
			else = { event_target:grain_store = { set_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 1 } } }
		}
		event_target:grain_store = { change_variable = { which = IR_price_mod value = 0.05 } change_variable = { which = IR_trading_number value = 1 } }
		#change_price = { trade_goods = grain key = COUNTRY_TRADING_IN value = 0.05 duration = 364 } 
	}
